  <h3 class="green">Login for <b>FREE</b> access</h3><div class="js-form-item form-item js-form-type-textfield form-type-textfield js-form-item-name form-item-name form-no-label">
      <label for="edit-name" class="visually-hidden js-form-required form-required">User Name/Email</label>
        <input autocorrect="none" autocapitalize="none" spellcheck="false" data-drupal-selector="edit-name" placeholder="Email" type="text" id="edit-name" name="name" value="" size="60" maxlength="60" class="form-text required" required="required" aria-required="true" />

<div id="block-tableexplanationfreestatsnflmaindrivestats" class="block block-region-footer_outside block-type-table_info">
  <a class="table-info-trigger">
    <span>This table explained</span> <i class="fa fa-plus"></i> <i class="fa fa-minus" style="display: none;"></i>
  </a>
  <div class="table-info-content" style="display: none;">
    
        
          
            <div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field__item"><p><em>Database updated: 1/04/2021 1:01 PM EST</em></p>
<p>These stats are computed from NFL Drive Charts and are not adjusted for strength of schedule or situation.</p>
<p><b>DSR</b> represents Drive Success Rate, as introduced in <i>Pro Football Prospectus 2005</i>, which measures the percentage of down series that result in a first down or touchdown. <b>TO/Dr</b> represents turnovers per drive. <b>FUM/Dr</b> represents fumbles lost per drive. <b>LOS/Dr</b> represents average starting field position (line of scrimmage) per drive. <b>TOP/Dr</b> represents time of possession per drive.</p>
<p>Take-a-knee drives at the end of a half are discarded. <b>NET</b> values are simply <b>OFFENSE</b> minus <b>DEFENSE.</b></p>
<p>Drive and pace stats are compiled by Jim Armstrong.</p>
</div>
